                Coronavirus: China’s belt and road plan hits roadblock as virus pinches supply of materials and workers
            </h1><div class="info__subHeadline" data-v-0ff1f739><div data-v-0ff1f739><ul class="generic-article__summary--ul content--ul" data-v-e4bae94c data-v-0ff1f739>
<li class="generic-article__summary--li content--li" data-v-e4bae94c>Despite tentative signs of economic recovery at home, projects under the Belt and Road Initiative remain cut off from vital Chinese materials and specialist labour</li>
<li class="generic-article__summary--li content--li" data-v-e4bae94c>Supply chain disruptions are pushing out existing project timelines, including in Indonesia, Pakistan and Bangladesh, and adding uncertainty to new plans</li>
